    if($.cookie("auth0_redir") !== undefined){
        let cookie = $.cookie('auth0_redir').split('?')[0]
        
        if(cookie){
            let url_string = window.location.href
            let url = new URL(url_string)
            let code = url.searchParams.get('code')
            let state = url.searchParams.get('state')

            let URLdomain = ".ole.com.ar"
            
            if(!url_string.includes("//www.ole.com.ar")){
                URLdomain = "prepro-ole.int.clarin.com"
            }

            $.removeCookie('auth0_redir', {
                path: '/',
                domain: URLdomain
            });

            location.href = cookie + '?code='+ code + '&state=' + state;
        }
    }
</script>

    function getMetricsCookie(name){
        
        var dc      = document.cookie;
        var prefix  = name + "=";
        var begin   = dc.indexOf("; " + prefix);
        
        if(begin == -1){
            begin = dc.indexOf(prefix);
            if (begin != 0){
                return null;
            } 
        } 
        else{
            begin += 2;
        }
        
        var end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", begin);
        if(end == -1){
            end = dc.length;
        }
        
        return unescape(dc.substring(begin + prefix.length, end));
    }

    function deleteMetricsCookie(name, path, domain){
        
        if (getMetricsCookie(name)){
            
            document.cookie = name + "=" +
            ((path) ? "; path=" + path : "") +
            ((domain) ? "; domain=" + domain : "") +
            "; expires=Thu, 01-Jan-70 00:00:01 GMT";
        }
    }

    var daxRefresh = "&refresh=no";

    if(getMetricsCookie("desMetricsRefresh") == 1){
	   
       deleteMetricsCookie("desMetricsRefresh");
	   daxRefresh = "&refresh=si";
    }	

    function getIdPase() {
        
        var idPase = $.cookie('idPase');

        if (idPase != null && idPase != "") {
            return idPase;
        } else {
            return "";
        }
    }

    function getIdPaseToStringUrl () {

        var idPase = getIdPase();
        
        if (idPase != "" ) {
            return "&pase_id=" + idPase;
        } else {
            return "";
        }
    }

    'getParameterLWtoDax' : function(){

        var params = '';
        var lwm_count_sum = 0;
        var lwm_blocked = "no";

        if($.cookie('lw-tracking-olev2')){

            var oData = JSON.parse($.cookie('lw-tracking-olev2'));
            lwm_count_sum = oData.urls.length;
            lwm_blocked = (oData.isBlocked) ? "si" : "no";
        }

        params += "&lwm_count=no";
        params += "&lwm_count_sum=" + lwm_count_sum;
        params += "&lwm_block=no";
        params += "&lwm_blocked=" +lwm_blocked;

        return params;

    }
};

<script type="text/javascript">

    function getGenDate(value) {
        var nombre = $.cookie('idPase');
        if(nombre != null){
            var cookieValue = $.cookie(value);

            if(cookieValue != null) {
                return cookieValue;
            }
        }
        return 0;
    }

    function getLWCount() {
        var cookieData = $.cookie('lw-tracking-olev2');
        var oData = {};
        if(cookieData != '' && cookieData != null){
            oData = JSON.parse(cookieData);
        }
        return typeof(oData.urls) == 'undefined' ? 0 : oData.urls.length;
    }

    function getAge() {
        if(getGenDate("Pase-fecNac")){
            var today = new Date();
            var birthDate = new Date(getGenDate("Pase-fecNac"));
            var age = today.getFullYear() - birthDate.getFullYear();
            var m = today.getMonth() - birthDate.getMonth();
            if (m < 0 || (m === 0 && today.getDate() < birthDate.getDate())) {
                age--;
            }
            return age.toString();
        }
        return "";
    }

    function getKwPw() {
        // console.log(document.cookie);
        // console.log("pase");
        var _user = WAuth.getUserSync();
        if (_user != "null" && _user != null){
            if(_user.subscriptionStatus == "not_subscribed") {
                return 1;
            } else if(_user.subscriptionStatus == "subscribed") {
                return 2;
            }
            else{
                return 0;
            }
        }
        else
            return 0;
    }

    function getPwChoque() {

        if($.cookie('paywall-choque')){
            return $.cookie('paywall-choque');
        } else {
            setCookie('paywall-choque', 0);
        }

        return $.cookie('paywall-choque');
    }

    function setCookie(name, value, params){
        params = params || {};
        var defaultParams = {
            path: '/',
            domain: '.ole.com'
        };
        $.extend(defaultParams, params);
        return $.cookie(name, value, defaultParams);
    }
    var adskv =  {

        'kw_pw_counter': [getLWCount().toString()],
        'kw_time': [Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000).toString()],
        'kw_temperatura': [],
        'kw_pw': [getKwPw()],
        'kw_choque': [getPwChoque()],
        'kw_login_edad': [],
        'kw_login_sexo': []
    }

        });

    function cerrar2() {
        document.getElementById("b-main-top").style.display='none';

    myID = document.getElementById("b-main-top");
    
    var myScrollFunc = function () {
        var y = window.scrollY;
        if (y >= 100) {
            myID.className = "b-visible"
        } else {
            myID.className = "b-hidden"
        }
    };
    
    window.addEventListener("scroll", myScrollFunc);

<script type="text/javascript">
        // debounce function that will wrap our event
        function debounce(fn, delay) {
          // maintain a timer
          let timer = null;
          // closure function that has access to timer
          return function() {
            // get the scope and parameters of the function 
            // via 'this' and 'arguments'
            let context = this;
            let args = arguments;
            // if event is called, clear the timer and start over
            clearTimeout(timer);
            timer = setTimeout(function() {
              fn.apply(context, args);
            }, delay);
          }
        }
        schneiderBannerAlreadySeen = false;
        function isSchneiderBannerScrolledIntoView()
        {
            if (!schneiderBannerAlreadySeen) {
                var elem = $("#homeBannerSchneider");
                if (elem.length == 0) {
                     window.removeEventListener('scroll', isSchneiderBannerScrolledIntoView);
                    return true;
                }
                var docViewTop = $(window).scrollTop();
                var docViewBottom = docViewTop + $(window).height();

                var elemTop = $(elem).offset().top;
                var elemBottom = elemTop + $(elem).height();

                if ((elemBottom <= docViewBottom) && (elemTop >= docViewTop)) {
                    schneiderBannerAlreadySeen = true;
                    window.removeEventListener('scroll', isSchneiderBannerScrolledIntoView);
                    var script = document.createElement("script");
                    script.lang = "JavaScript1.1";
                    script.src = "https://ad.doubleclick.net/ddm/trackimpj/N249001.2284904OL/B21937119.234787293;dc_trk_aid=432339691;dc_trk_cid=83358429;ord=[timestamp];dc_lat=;dc_rdid=;tag_for_child_directed_treatment=;tfua=?"; 
                    document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
                    return true;
                } else {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
        window.addEventListener('scroll', debounce(isSchneiderBannerScrolledIntoView, 200));
    </script>
<script type="text/javascript">
                $(window).on("keydown", function(e) {
                    if (e.which == 27) {
                        $('.popup-close').click();
                    }
                });
                var lastElement = $(".on-demand").last().index();
                var el = $(".on-demand").first();
                // "false" - El funcionamiento de la pagina es scroll a demanda del usuario.
                // "true" -  Los scroll se cargan automaticamente.
                var autoLoadScroll = true;

                $(document).ready(function(){
                    if(lastElement != -1) {
                        $('footer').hide();
                    }
                });

                function getOnDemandNumber(){
                    var cantidad_total = $(".on-demand").length;
                    $(".on-demand").each(function(index){
                        if ($(this).html() == '') {
                            cantidad_total--;
                        }
                    });  
                    return cantidad_total + 1;                  
                }

                var updateOnDemand = function(e) {
                    $(window).unbind("scroll.OnDemand");
                    var index_scroll = getOnDemandNumber();
                   // uid_call("web.home.scroll-on-demand."+index_scroll, "event");
                    try{
                        $.ajax({
                            type: 'GET',
                            url: e.data("src"),
                            beforeSend: function(){
                                e.html('<div class="demand-loading"><div class=centerLoading><img src="/static/OLEOleV2/images/loading.gif"><p>Cargando...</p></div></div>');
                            },
                            complete: function(_response){

                                if (typeof BBT == "undefined"){return;}
                                response = BBT.fixJson(_response['responseText']);
                                if(!response){
                                    return;
                                }
                                if (response.error == 0) {
                                    e.html(response.data);
                                    e.find(".sticky-spacer > [data-stick]").stickAll();
                                    if(lastElement!=-1){
                                        if ( e.index() != lastElement ) {
                                            el = e.next(".on-demand");
                                            updateBody();
                                            if (typeof ads != "undefined") {
                                                ads.pending();
                                            } 
                                        }else{
                                            $('footer').show();
                                        }
                                    }else{
                                        $('footer').show();
                                    }
                                    
                                    OLE.Modules.initialize();
                                    initVideos();
                                }
                            }
                        });
                    }catch(err){
                        console.log("on demand Error: "+err);
                    }   
                }

                function checkScroll(e) {
                    
                    var altoScroll = $('body').height() - $('footer').height();;
                    var porcCargaScroll = altoScroll - ($(window).height() + 50 );
                    
                    if ($(window).scrollTop() >= porcCargaScroll){
                        updateOnDemand(e);
                    }
                }

                function updateBody () {
                    if(autoLoadScroll)
                    {
                        checkScroll(el);
                        updateOnDemand(el);
                    }else{
                        if ($(window).height() >= $("body").height() ) {
                            updateOnDemand(el);
                        } else {
                            $('footer').hide();
                            $(window).bind("scroll.OnDemand", function(){
                                checkScroll(el);
                            })
                        }
                    }
                }

                var twtScript = document.createElement("script");
                twtScript.type = "text/javascript";
                twtScript.src = "//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js";
                $("head").append(twtScript);

                $(document).ready(function() {
                    if($("body").height() < $(window).height()) {
                        updateOnDemand(el);
                    }
                });

                if ( typeof el.html() != "undefined" ){
                    updateBody();
                }
            </script>

<script type="application/javascript">
    function GDPRInit() {
        var scriptJS = document.createElement('script');
        if(scriptJS.readyState) {
            scriptJS.onreadystatechange = function() {
                if ( scriptJS.readyState === "loaded" || scriptJS.readyState === "complete" ) {
                    scriptJS.onreadystatechange = null;
                    GDPRStart()
                }
            };
        } else{
            // others
            scriptJS.onload = function() {
                GDPRStart()
            }
        }
        scriptJS.src = "/commons/js/GDPRCookiePolicy.js";
        document.documentElement.appendChild(scriptJS);
    }
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
$(".terminos").click(function(){
    OLE.Popup.open('DAt');
    try{
        $.ajax({
            type: 'GET',
            url: '/oleolev2/politica-de-proteccion-de-datos.html',
            beforeSend: function(){
                $("#DAt .popup-content").html('<img class="loadTerm" src="/static/OLEOleV2/images/loading.gif">');
            },
            complete: function(_response){
                if (typeof BBT == "undefined"){
                    return;
                }

                response = BBT.fixJson(_response['responseText']);
                if(!response){
                    return;
                }
                if (response.error == 0) {
                    $(".loadTerm").remove();
                    $(".dataTerminos").html(response['data']);
                }
            },
        });
    }catch(err){
        console.log("Ajax Error: "+err);
    }

});

$(".normas").click(function(){
    OLE.Popup.open('DAt');
    try{
        $.ajax({
            type: 'GET',
            url: '/oleolev2/normas-de-privacidad-y-confidencialidad.html',
            beforeSend: function(){
                $("#DAt .popup-content").html('<img class="loadTerm" src="/static/OLEOleV2/images/loading.gif">');
            },
            complete: function(_response){
                if (typeof BBT == "undefined"){
                    return;
                }

                response = BBT.fixJson(_response['responseText']);
                if(!response){
                    return;
                }
                if (response.error == 0) {
                    $(".loadTerm").remove();
                    $(".dataTerminos").html(response['data']);
                }
            },
        });
    }catch(err){
        console.log("Ajax Error: "+err);
    }

});

$(window).load(function() {
    /* detección de footer */
    var footerPosition = $(document).height() - $(".site-footer").height(),
        timeout = null,
        tracked_footer = false,
        tracked_temas = false;

    if ($("#temas_section").length > 0){
        var temasPosition = $("#temas_section").offset().top;
    }
    $(window).scroll(function (){
        var scrollBottomOfThePage = $(window).scrollTop() + $(window).height();
        if (!tracked_footer){
            if($('footer').css('display') != "none"){
                footerPosition = $(document).height() - $(".site-footer").height();
                if (scrollBottomOfThePage >= footerPosition) {
                    tracked_footer = true;
                  //  uid_call("web.footer", "event");
                }
            }
        }
        if (!tracked_temas && temasPosition){
            if (scrollBottomOfThePage >= temasPosition) {
                tracked_temas = true;
               // uid_call("web.findenota", "event");
            }
        }
    });

});

$(document).ready(function() {
    $(".newsletter-subscribe").click(function() {
        if($.cookie('idPase')) {
            $("#mis-preferencias").click();
            return false;
        } else {
            $(paseE2E.settings.placeIngresar+':eq(0)').click();
            return false;
        }
    });

   /* $(".footer-link").click(function() {
        var link_desc = $(this).attr('data-dax');
        uid_call("web.footer.link." + link_desc, "click");
    });*/

    $(".related-link").click(function() {
        var link_aux = $(this).attr('data-dax');
        var link_desc = "";
        if (link_aux.indexOf("-")>0){
            link_aux = link_aux.split("-");
            if (link_aux[0]=='sum1'){
                link_desc = "orden." + ((parseInt(link_aux[1]))+1);
            }else{
                link_desc = "orden."+link_aux[1];
            }
        }else{
            link_desc = link_aux;
        }
      //  uid_call("web.relacionada." + link_desc, "click");
    });


});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    
    function initVideos () {
        if ( $(".genoaPlayer").length > 0) {
            $.each($(".genoaPlayer"), function (index, value) {
                renderGenoaMultimedia(value);
            });
        }
    }

    function renderGenoaMultimedia(value) {
        var iframe = getPlayerIframe( $(value));
        $(value).replaceWith(iframe);
    }

    function getPlayerIframe(elm){
        var params = {
            url: elm.attr('data-src'),
            playerId: elm.attr('data-player'),
            width: elm.attr('data-width'),
            height: elm.attr('data-height'),
            scrolling: elm.attr('data-scrolling'),
            frameborder: elm.attr('data-frameborder'),
            allowfullscreen: elm.attr('data-allowfullscreen')
        };

        var genoaPvastEncoded = getGenoaPvast();
        
        if ($(".intVideoTpl").length > 0
         || $(".oletevedestacada").length > 0
         || $(".oletevesumario").length > 0) {
            if (1 !== 1) {
                params.width = "1000px";
                params.height = "562px";
            }
        }

        var iframe = $('<iframe>', {
            scrolling: params.scrolling,
            frameborder: params.frameborder,
            allowfullscreen: params.allowfullscreen,
            width: params.width,
            height: params.height,
            src: params.url + genoaPvastEncoded
        });

        return iframe;
    }


    function isFacebookApp() {
        var ua = navigator.userAgent || navigator.vendor || window.opera;
        return (ua.indexOf("FBAN") > -1) || (ua.indexOf("FBAV") > -1);
    }

    function getAge(dateString) {
        var age = "-2";
        if (dateString) {
            var today = new Date();
            var birthDate = new Date(dateString);
            var age = today.getFullYear() - birthDate.getFullYear();
            var m = today.getMonth() - birthDate.getMonth();
            if (m < 0 || (m === 0 && today.getDate() < birthDate.getDate())) {
                age--;
            }
        }
        return age;
    }

    function getGenoaPvast() {

        var genoaVars = [];

        /*if(localStorage.getItem('fbtoken')) {
            genoaVars.push('fan='+localStorage.getItem('fbtoken'));
        } else {
            genoaVars.push('fan=-2');
        }*/
        if(["0","1"].includes(localStorage.getItem('fbfan'))) {
            genoaVars.push('kw_fan='+localStorage.getItem('fbfan'));
        } else {
            genoaVars.push('kw_fan=-2');
        }

        /*if(typeof $('#page-data')  != 'undefined') {
            var pageData = $('#page-data').data();
            for (var key in pageData) {
                if (pageData.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
                    genoaVars.push(key + '=' + pageData[key]);
                }
            }
        }
        
        if (isFacebookApp()) {
            IdPase = paseE2E.idPase;
        } else {
            IdPase = paseE2E.getCookie("idPase");
        }
        if(paseE2E && typeof IdPase !== "undefined" && IdPase !== "" && IdPase !== null){
            genoaVars.push('pase_id=' + IdPase);
            genoaVars.push('pase_sexo=' + paseE2E.getCookie("Pase-genero"));
            genoaVars.push('pase_edad=' + getAge(paseE2E.getCookie("Pase-fecNac")));
        } else {
            genoaVars.push('pase_id=-2');
            genoaVars.push('pase_sexo=-2');
            genoaVars.push('pase_edad=-2');
        }*/

        var genoaPvast = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < genoaVars.length; i ++) {
            if(i>0) {
                genoaPvast += '&';
            }
            genoaPvast += genoaVars[i];
        }
        genoaPvastEncoded = '';
        if(genoaPvast != '') {
            // se comenta ya que más adelante se va a implementar de esta forma el desarrollo
            genoaPvastEncoded = '?pvast='+encodeURIComponent('cust_params='+encodeURIComponent(genoaPvast));
        }
        return genoaPvastEncoded;
    }
</script>
